# CONSTANT FOR Minor Parties TIMES (These needs to be x7 compared to the Focus cost in the focus file) - NEEDS TO MATCH THE SAME CONSTANTS USED IN THE FOCUS FILE x7
@HOL_D66_time_tier_1 = 210
# FLAG CONSTANTS (It is 1 day more so the tooltip and days shown in the focus about Focus Progress match exactly the moment when the focus is completed)
@HOL_D66_time_tier_1_flag = 211

#Economy Events
country_event = {
	id = HOL_economy.001 #Borsele
	title = HOL_economy.001.t
	desc = HOL_economy.001.d
	picture = GFX_hol_borsele_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		#Nuclear
		name = HOL_economy.001.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.001.a executed"
		47 = {
			one_state_nuclear_reactor = yes
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Coal
		name = HOL_economy.001.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.001.b executed"
		47 = {
			two_state_fossil_fuel_powerplant = yes
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = HOL_economy.002 #Wunderline Request to Germany
	title = HOL_economy.002.t
	desc = HOL_economy.002.d
	#picture = GFX_hol_wunderline_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = HOL_economy.002.a #accept
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.002.a executed"
		HOL = { country_event = HOL_economy.003 }
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.05 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = HOL_economy.002.b #reject
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.002.b executed"
		HOL = { country_event = HOL_economy.004 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				GER = { is_puppet_of = HOL }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = HOL_economy.021 #Building ASML in Foreign Countries
	title = HOL_economy.021.t
	desc = HOL_economy.021.d
	picture = GFX_hol_asml_building_abroad_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = HOL_economy.021.a #Accept
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.021.a executed"
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				random_owned_state = {
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							add_building_construction = {
								type = offices
								level = 1
								instant_build = yes
							}
							set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -13 }
							modify_treasury_effect = yes
						}
						50 = {
							add_building_construction = {
								type = industrial_complex
								level = 1
								instant_build = yes
							}
							add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
							set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -8.5 }
							modify_treasury_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			30 = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = HOL_ASML_Tech
					category = CAT_3d
					category = CAT_computing_tech
					bonus = 0.50
					uses = 1
				}
			}
		}
		HOL = { country_event = HOL_economy.022 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = HOL_economy.021.b #Refuse
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_economy.021.b executed"
		HOL = { country_event = HOL_economy.023 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				is_puppet_of = HOL
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

					instant_build = yes

			}

				limit = { has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny" }

					add_mio_funds = 1000
				}
			}
		}

			base = 50
		}

country_event = {
	id = HOL_military.032 #Cashback event Airbus
	title = HOL_military.032.t
	desc = HOL_military.032.d
	picture = GFX_airbus_transport_airplane_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.032.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.032.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = HOL_accepts_mrtt
					has_country_flag = BEL_accepts_mrtt
					has_country_flag = LUX_accepts_mrtt
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 7.5 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = { has_country_flag = HOL_accepts_mrtt has_country_flag = BEL_accepts_mrtt }
						AND = { has_country_flag = HOL_accepts_mrtt has_country_flag = LUX_accepts_mrtt }
						AND = { has_country_flag = BEL_accepts_mrtt has_country_flag = HOL_accepts_mrtt }
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 4.5 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_hol_future_air_defender_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = HOL_germany_scrapped_FAD
		has_country_flag = HOL_sweden_rejected_FAD
		has_country_flag = HOL_denmark_rejected_FAD
		has_country_flag = HOL_norway_rejected_FAD
	}

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.048.a # Invest more and start building two ships
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.048.a executed"
		add_equipment_production = {
			equipment = {
				type = frigate_hull_5
				version_name = "Future Air Defender"
			}
			amount = 2
			progress = 0.33
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -35 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				gdp_debt_ratio_higher_70 = yes
				add = -60
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = HOL_military.048.b # Scrap the project
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.048.b executed"
		set_technology = { FAD_access_tech = 0 }
		add_equipment_production = {
			equipment = {
				type = frigate_hull_5
				version_name = "Future Air Defender"
			}
			amount = -2
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

	desc = HOL_military.065.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_stealth_destroyer
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = HOL_military.60_bonus
				bonus = 0.15
				uses = 1
				technology = stealth_destroyer_hull_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				NOT = { is_special_project_completed = sp:sp_stealth_destroyer }
			}
			add_breakthrough_points = {
				specialization = specialization_naval
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = HOL_military.60_bonus
				bonus = 0.15
				uses = 1
				technology = stealth_destroyer_1
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.065.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.065.b executed"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = HOL_destroyer_research

			uses = 1
			technology = destroyer_hull_4
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = HOL_military.066
	title = HOL_military.066.t
	desc = HOL_military.066.d
	picture = GFX_hol_marine_kazerne_event_picture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.066.a  # Support the Move
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.066.a executed"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = HOL_Marine_Moving
			add_idea = HOL_Marine_Debate  # Debate begins
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.08 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_the_military_opinion = yes
		country_event = { id = HOL_military.067 days = 180 }  # Trigger next event in 180 days
	}

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.066.b  # Reevaluate the Plan
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.066.b executed"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = HOL_Marine_Moving
			add_idea = HOL_Marine_Debate
		}
		add_stability = 0.08  # Government stability increases slightly
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.04 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -2 }
		change_the_military_opinion = yes
		country_event = { id = HOL_military.068 days = 180 }  # Trigger next event in 180 days
	}

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.066.c  # Cancel the Move
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.066.c executed"
		remove_ideas = HOL_Marine_Moving
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = HOL_Marine_Relocation_Cancelled
			days = 365
		}
		add_stability = 0.05  # Gain stability from cancellation
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
		change_the_military_opinion = yes
	}
}

			add_equipment_production = {
				equipment = {
				type = missile_frigate_4
				version_name = "Vlissingenklasse"
				}
				industrial_manufacturer = mio:FRA_naval_group_naval_manufacturer
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_the_military_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_defense_industry_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_per_capita }
		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.15 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = HOL_military.083
	title = HOL_military.083.t
	desc = HOL_military.083.d
	picture = GFX_hol_army_bad_state_event_picture


	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = HOL_military.083.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: HOL_military.083.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army5 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army5
				add_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army4
				add_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army3
				add_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army2
				add_idea = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army1
			}
		}
		add_ideas = HOL_nonselfsufficient_army_emergency
	}
}

				has_shine_effect_on_focus = HOL_gl_transparent_governance
			}
			complete_national_focus = {
				focus = HOL_gl_transparent_governance
				use_side_message = yes
				originator_name = Neutral_green_L
			}
			clr_country_flag = HOL_GL_in_progress_flag
			country_event = { id = HOL_politics.61 days = HOL_minor_parties_to_start_focus random_days = HOL_minor_parties_random_days }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_shine_effect_on_focus = HOL_gl_youth_empowerment
			}
			complete_national_focus = {
				focus = HOL_gl_youth_empowerment
				use_side_message = yes
				originator_name = Neutral_green_L
			}
			clr_country_flag = HOL_GL_in_progress_flag
			country_event = { id = HOL_politics.61 days = HOL_minor_parties_to_start_focus random_days = HOL_minor_parties_random_days }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_shine_effect_on_focus = HOL_gl_energy_independence
			}
			complete_national_focus = {
				focus = HOL_gl_energy_independence
				use_side_message = yes
				originator_name = Neutral_green_L
			}
			clr_country_flag = HOL_GL_in_progress_flag
			country_event = { id = HOL_politics.61 days = HOL_minor_parties_to_start_focus random_days = HOL_minor_parties_random_days }
		}
	}
}
